 excludedCalendarDays.push(6);

 if (jQuery.inArray(date.getDay(), excludedCalendarDays) != -1) {

 excludedDates[i] = new Date(excludedDates[i]).toString();

 return [false, '', ''];
 }
 }
 return [true, '', ''];
 });
